Proto Definition\n- **`api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto`**\n  - Defines `HeaderInjectionRule` message with:\n    - `header_name`: The name of the header to inject\n    - `header_value`: The value to inject\n    - `inject_in_request`: Whether to inject in requests\n    - `inject_in_response`: Whether to inject in responses\n  - Defines `CustomHeaderInjection` for filter configuration\n  - Defines `CustomHeaderInjectionPerRoute` for per-route configuration\n  - Follows Envoy extension naming convention\n\n- **`api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/BUILD`**\n  - Bazel build configuration for proto files\n\n### 2. Filter Implementation\n\n#### Header File\n- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h`**\n  - `CustomHeaderInjectionConfig`: Filter configuration class\n    - Inherits from `Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig`\n    - Parses and stores header injection rules\n  - `PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection`: Per-route configuration class\n  - `CustomHeaderInjectionFilter`: Main filter class\n    - Inherits from `Http::PassThroughFilter` and `Logger::Loggable`\n    - Implements `decodeHeaders()` for request header injection\n    - Implements `encodeHeaders()` for response header injection\n    - Private `injectHeaders()` helper method\n\n#### Implementation File\n- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc`**\n  - Constructor initializes configuration from proto\n  - `decodeHeaders()`: Processes request headers, returns `FilterHeadersStatus::Continue`\n  - `encodeHeaders()`: Processes response headers, returns `FilterHeadersStatus::Continue`\n  - `injectHeaders()`: Conditionally adds headers based on rules\n    - Respects `inject_in_request` and `inject_in_response` flags\n    - Uses `Http::LowerCaseString` for proper header handling\n    - Uses `headers.setCopy()` to set header values\n\n### 3. Factory Configuration\n\n#### Header File\n- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h`**\n  - `CustomHeaderInjectionFactoryConfig`: Factory class\n    - Inherits from `Common::DualFactoryBase` to support both global and per-route configs\n    - Filter name: \"envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection\"\n    - Declares `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` for filter instantiation\n    - Declares `createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped()` for per-route configs\n\n#### Implementation File\n- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc`**\n  - Implements factory methods\n  - Creates shared configuration from proto\n  - Returns filter factory callback\n  - Registers factory with `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro\n\n### 4. Bazel Build Files\n\n- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/BUILD`**\n  - Defines `filter_lib` target with filter implementation\n  - Defines `config` target with factory registration\n  - Includes dependencies on proto, HTTP interfaces, and utilities\n\n- **`test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/BUILD`**\n  - Defines `filter_test` target\n  - Specifies extension registration for tests\n\n### 5. Test Implementation\n\n- **`test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc`**\n  - `CustomHeaderInjectionTest` test class\n  - Tests for request header injection\n  - Tests for response header injection\n  - Tests for combined request+response injection\n  - Tests for multiple headers with different configurations\n  - Uses mock filter callbacks\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Filter Lifecycle\n\n1. **Configuration Loading**: Factory creates `CustomHeaderInjectionConfig` from proto\n2. **Request Phase**:\n   - `decodeHeaders()` is called with request headers\n   - Filter injects headers where `inject_in_request` is true\n   - Returns `Continue` to pass to next filter\n3. **Response Phase**:\n   - `encodeHeaders()` is called with response headers\n   - Filter injects headers where `inject_in_response` is true\n   - Returns `Continue` to pass to next filter\n\n### Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Inheritance from `Http::PassThroughFilter`**: Provides default implementations for all filter methods not overridden\n2. **Dual Factory Support**: Uses `DualFactoryBase` to support both global and per-route configurations\n3. **Simple Rule Structure**: Each rule specifies exact header name and value\n4. **Conditional Injection**: Rules include flags to control whether headers are injected in requests, responses, or both\n\n## Success Criteria Met\n\n✅ Filter header file declares class inheriting from StreamDecoderFilter/StreamEncoderFilter\n✅ Filter implementation has decodeHeaders/encodeHeaders methods\n✅ Factory config file registers the filter\n✅ Follows Envoy naming: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection\n✅ Test file exists with comprehensive test cases\n✅ Proto definition created with proper message structure\n✅ BUILD files properly configured for bazel build system\n✅ All files follow Envoy code conventions and patterns\n\n## Configuration Example\n\n```yaml\nfilters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection\n  config:\n    headers:\n    - header_name: X-Custom-Request\n      header_value: request-value\n      inject_in_request: true\n      inject_in_response: false\n    - header_name: X-Custom-Response\n      header_value: response-value\n      inject_in_request: false\n      inject_in_response: true\n    - header_name: X-Custom-Both\n      header_value: both-value\n      inject_in_request: true\n      inject_in_response: true\n```\n\n## Per-Route Configuration Example\n\n```yaml\nroute_config:\n  routes:\n  - match:\n      prefix: \"/api\"\n    route:\n      cluster: backend\n    typed_per_filter_config:\n      envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection:\n        headers:\n        - header_name: X-Route-Specific\n          header_value: route-value\n          inject_in_request: true\n          inject_in_response: true\n```\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":507,"cache_read_input_tokens":86742,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":507},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"933ba2b0-a07c-40e6-b563-85d9a3f5a5a9","uuid":"49fe169f-56ac-4d24-88a6-435e667c3000"}
